I swung by here right before closing time to basically kill time in a fun way for my twin 10 yr old boys. When I noticed they were just a few minutes from closing, I figured we would just eyeball a few cool looking reptiles and then get out in time for them to lock up.

We looked around a bit & despite the time, a gentleman asked if we needed any help. Even after telling him that I was using their facility as a quick, free mini-zoo (loser parent in for the win) he graciously and patiently shared his knowledge with my boys and me. He even opened another area to show us more & let my twins pet one of the monitors (biggest reptile they've ever touched) and hold a couple snakes! His casual & comfortable nature helped dispel any preconceived fears of snakes and large reptiles. All this while understanding that I wasn't there to buy anything. We never felt rushed to get out (my own guilt for keeping him there was pushing us to leave).

All of the pets awaiting homes were well taken care of & the place was very clean. No telltale sign by means of odor that there were dozens of reptiles inside.

If I EVER decide to get a reptile, it will be from here, where I know the reptile has been kept healthy & they'll spend the time educating their customer.</text>

< Review>
Fantastic sandwich shop in Folsom! Their signature, Mr Pickle, is an amazing combo of fresh avocado, Crispy bacon, and grilled chicken all warm and smothered in goodness.

Not sold yet? Than how about a free, delicious, fresh baked chocolate chip cookie with your meal?

Still not sold? Wow. You are tough. They also carry the best potato chips I've ever had. Dirty Potato Chips and the Funky Fusion flavor is...unparalleled.

It does get pretty busy at lunch times, but well worth the wait - or order ahead and take it to go!</Review>

<text>I'm 35 years old, and I've never been in a sandwich shop with worse customer service than this joke of a restaurant. On two occasions, I have placed to-go orders for a signature Mr. Pickle sandwich. The first time, I got there about 10 minutes after my call, and I had to wait another 15 minutes before I got the sandwich. They were busy, so I excused it.

The second time, the man on the phone said they could have it ready in five minutes. I get over there about 10 minutes later. Still not done. Someone asks me if I want the sandwich for there or to go. I tell them to go. I wait several more minutes, and the sandwich is still not done, despite the fact that the people behind the counter outnumber the measly amount of customers in the restaurant. So I left to go to Subway down the sidewalk.

I work at a job where I have to clock in and clock out, so I don't have the luxury of wasting time for people who mislead me about when my food will get done. Is the food at Mr. Pickle better than Subway's? Sure. But what difference does it make when you're lied to on the phone and when the staff can't even make the restaurant's signature sandwich in a timely manner?</text>< name>

< Text>
Thank you Juan and the staff for being so accommodating to us this evening. The restaurant was hosting a private event unbeknownst a nosotros. We arrived ten minutes before close, looking for some tacos after seeing the good recommendations on yelp. I would have completely understood being turned away at the door under these circumstances however Juan received us with open arms. While we waited for whatever tacos were available, Juan offered us complimentary beverages, bbq chicken, and ribs. Wow! They had been smoking the meats out back, though We now know they have a bbq every Sunday from 10:30am -1pm. We'll be sure to come back for that, as well as check out their other location in Santa Monica.

I am completely shocked at the monumental generosity of this place. You will be hard pressed to find such hospitality these days in this city or anywhere.</Text>

1. I‚Äôm in a rush, give me a one sentence summary ‚Äì affordable and quality cuts of meat, perfect for grilling or preparing for dinner.

2. The carniceria ‚Äì my review only pertains to the carniceria, as I never have eaten at the restaurant which is attached to this market. I come to the carniceria to pick up meat for grilling and pan searing for tacos, and have always been able to find affordable and quality cuts of meat. My favorite are the al pastor ($3.99/lb), chicken fajitas ($2.99/lb), and chorizo ($2.99/lb). They also have a wide variety of cuts.

3. 5 stars off for cleanliness ‚Äì they have an open doorway and (I think) keep the back door open as well to provide circulation since they have no air conditioning, so I usually see flies and other bugs zooming around. Not the most appealing sight when I‚Äôm trying to buy food which can be exposed to these bugs.

4. Location/parking ‚Äì It can be easy to overlook, as it‚Äôs right on the corner of Sawtelle & Washington Pl. after you exit the 405 at Venice. They have a 15 minute parking zone right in front of the restaurant on both sides which is very convenient and helpful, especially when coming right off the 405.< /review>

< Review>
Beautiful, thriving, little parish just north of Downtown Long Beach.

I like that the altar is traditional and all the masses are ad orientem, that is, facing towards the tabernacle rather than away from it. And the fact that the tabernacle is front and center is a big plus; not to mention the communion rails and the more traditional method of giving communion. Good, good.

Fr Irving is a wonderful pastor, may the Lord grant him a long and spiritually fruitful life.< /Review>

I don't even know where to begin...2 weeks ago we purchased a sofa that was supposed to be delivered today. I thought it was strange that she told as one sofa was in stock because a prior employee told us it was back ordered, but she said the prior employee didn't know what he was talking about. She even suggested we finance the couch at 0% for 12 months so we thought it was a great deal. I never take store credit but in this case I made an exception even though I knew that doing so would lower my credit score slightly since its a hard credit pull, but I figured at the time it was a good deal because I was expecting to receive my sofa yesterday and pay it off in 12 months. Fast forward to the day of our delivery date, both my husband and I receive texts, phone calls, and emails two days and the day prior of our delivery date confirming our delivery and were even given a time frame. We took the day off from work to wait for the delivery and waited the entire delivery hour window and no show. No phone call from the company either. A technician was sent to my home 23 days later and confirmed the motor to be replaced. Middle of September, however, a bulky wrong ‚Äòchair part‚Äô was delivered and the Warranty Service sent me an email saying they had placed a new order of the ‚Äòright part‚Äô on Oct. 1.

If the part arrives in 12 weeks, and another 3 weeks  to get the motor replaced, it will be middle of January next year, a whooping FIVE MONTHS after the claim was filed.

Be aware of the warranty service on items Living Spaces sells. They are dragging their feet and numerous calls have fallen to deaf ears. I spent over 30 hours to get the warranty service on repair, speaking to a host of incompetent and ill-trained reps including a couple of supervisors who lacked ‚Äòdue diligence‚Äô could not get the store to respond.

Finally after three months of nonsense, I had to revisit the store where a possible replacement could be found. None found. < Text>
Sorry this is long, but I hope helpful to some of you:

I went into this Living Spaces store and ordered two pieces -- a lamp and a TV stand -- to be delivered the following Tuesday. They have very broad delivery windows -- they won't be more specific than a 6 hour window when you book, and then they narrow it down to a still pretty broad 3 hour window the day before. I live on a narrow street in San Francisco, and so needed a small truck for the delivery, which was notated on the paperwork and in their system.

I need to be at work on Tuesday, but my Mom graciously agrees to wait at my place to take the delivery. They call me during my delivery window to tell me that even though the notes say they need a small truck, they didn't bring a small truck. Therefore they are unable to deliver the items that day. My Mom winds up waiting around my place for no reason. When they call, I ask when they can reschedule for, and they tell me they are a 3rd party contracted by Living Spaces and cannot help me with anything.

I call in and the first rep I speak with starts arguing with me about how it's not noted in the system that a small truck is needed. (It clearly was, I saw them do it when I was in the store, and it's on my paperwork.) She is so argumentative that she starts to get me agitated. I request a manager call back, which never happens.

I do get a call back from a non-manager to try and get me back on schedule. I agree to schedule for Saturday so I can be home to take delivery. They call me on Friday to tell me that they've misplaced the items -- items that were on their truck on Tuesday! They say they will keep looking for them and give me a call back one way or the other to let me know if they will be able to deliver. They never call. I call them Saturday morning and they still haven't located the items and can't make the delivery.

They call me back once again to try and reschedule. I tell them that I'm going to be out of town the next few weekends and at work during the week. In order to deliver, they will need to schedule me either first stop in the morning or in the early evening so I can meet them either before or after work. The person I speak with is understanding, and agrees that given that this is the 3rd time they are trying to deliver, they will go out of their way to make sure I'm first stop Thursday morning. He takes the time to talk to their dispatch supervisor to make sure this can be done.

I receive an email Wednesday saying that I'm now the 3rd stop, and scheduled for the middle of the day. I call in, get transferred to a supervisor, and am told that there's no way I can be the first stop. It does not work with their routing and not even the supervisor can control the routing. I tell the supervisor straight out that I'm not going to attempt a 4th delivery, and that they either hold up their promise for first stop Thursday or cancel my order. She cancels my order rather than accommodate me. This whole episode leaves me frustrated and angry. Not only are their operations horrible, but they just don't seem to care.

Reviews:
In-store experience: B+. I actually thought their store was nice and that their sales rep was helpful. I had to deal with a bad sales rep before I got a good one though.

Customer service experience: D. I spoke with one agent who was decent, but most just don't seem to care at all. Additionally, none of them seem to be empowered to help the customer in any way.

Delivery experience: F. They didn't read their notes about the small truck, and they misplaced my items when trying to deliver them the second time. They then decided not to accommodate me with the first stop even though it was noted. I know this is a third party contracted by Living Spaces, and if I were them I'd fire them and hire someone else.

Furniture: N/A. Never actually got my furniture because the other experiences were so bad.< /Text>

< Review>
One of the most ridiculous delivery experiences I've ever had. Which is a shame, because the in-store staff was helpful and the furniture itself seems nice.

I ordered a credenza on a Saturday, scheduled for delivery on Sunday morning. The delivery truck arrived Sunday with the wrong piece, so I sent it back and called to see when they could deliver the correct piece.  Twice I was told I'd receive a call from a manager which never came, and had to call back myself instead.

I was told by the first manager that I could get on the first delivery window for the next day (Monday), but then later a different manager told me I was on a later delivery window and that there was "nothing they could do" to affect who got on what delivery window or in what order.

I understand that trucks have to routed efficiently, and I understand why large delivery windows have to be given to account for variable delivery times. But when you've already screwed up by delivering the wrong piece, and are now forcing me to stay home from work on a Monday due to an error on your part, I would expect that they'd make some sort of effort to be accommodating. Instead it was literally just to the back of the queue like any other order.

I should say they did eventually say they would send me a $100 gift card for the trouble, which isn't very useful since I don't plan on shopping here again.< /Review>
